
Dayforce.Services Namespace
 
Interfaces

Interface
Description

IDayforceService
This interface defines the methods available on the Dayforce Services web service.

IDFNotificationReceiverService
This interface must be implemented by the notification receiver web service. Notification events will be published to the Receive method as events occur.

Employee's Citizenship

CloseReportPagesRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to close a previously executed report. This will clean-up all data stored on the server which will help alleviate performance and security issues. The response returned will be a CloseReportPagesResponse object.

CloseReportPagesResponse
This is the response resulting from submitting a CloseReportPagesRequest object. There is no data in the class, it merely represents that we received the request and have made out best efforts to clean up the report data.

Course
Employee's Course Information

Culture
Employee's Culture

DayforceServiceErrorCode
List of error codes that may be returned from Dayforce Services on the DFError class, Code property. The code provided in the documentation can be used if you need it in a client application. 
public class DayforceServiceErrorCode
{
    public static int None = 0;
    public static int UnexpectedError = 1000;
    public static int ConfigurationError = 1001;
    public static int AuthenticationError = 1002;
    public static int AuthorizationError = 1003;
    public static int ValidationError = 1004;
    public static int InvalidSessionError = 1005;
    public static int IpAddressRejected = 1006;
    public static int MaxRecordsExceeded = 1007;
}

DayforceServiceHiddenFromMetadataAttribute

Department
Employee's department information

DFAckNotificationRequest
Submit an instance of this class to DayforceServices.Query() method to acknowledge a collection of DFNotificationEvent objects.

DFAckNotificationResponse
This is the response resulting from submitting a DFAckNotificationRequest object. There is no data in the class, it merely represents that we received the request and have made out best efforts to clean up the report data.

DFAuthenticateResponse
Returned on a call to Authenticate and includes details about the session if one was created.

DFError
This is the standard error class that is returned on all Dayforce Service responses to inform the client if there was an error, and if so what the error was. 

DFGetClientSiteUriResponse
Returned on a call to GetClientSiteUri. This response includes information about where your requests should be submitted and the version of that target service.

DFNotificationAck
This is an acknowledgment class that should be returned upon receipt of a DFNotificationEvent instance. Once an ack is received, the DFNotificationEvent instance will be marked as successful and not sent again in the future.

DFNotificationData
This class is returned in response to submitting a DFNotificationDataRequest object. This class contains the data related to the event that has occurred.

DFNotificationDataRequest
Submit an instance of this class to DayforceServices.Query() method to retrieve a collection of DFNotificaitonData objects.

DFNotificationEvent
An instance of this class is sent to the notification receiver service to notify that an event has occured.

DFNotificationsRequest
Submit an instance of this class to DayforceServices.Query() method to retrieve a collection of DFNotificationEvent objects.

DFObject
Base class for all request and response objects used by Dayforce Services

DFRequest
Base class for all Request classes. Only classes that inherit from this class should be used as the second parameter of the external service methods.

DFResponse
Base class for all Response classes that return a single item.

DFResponseBase
Base call for all response classes. This base includes the DFError information to ensure all responses have that.

DFResponseList
Base class for all Response classes that return an array of items.

DirectDeposit
Employee's direct deposit information

DocMgmtSecurityGroup
Employee's Document Management Security Group

EIRate

EIRateInfo

GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employees that match a collection of XRefCodes. The results of this query request will be limited in number by the governor setting which is set at 1,000 employees.

GetEmployeesRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employees. The properties on this class are used as filters in the query to restrict the number of employees in the result. The results of this query request will be limited in number by the governor setting which is set at 1,000 employees.

GetEmployeeXRefCodesRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employee XRefCodes. This class differs from GetEmployeesRequest in that the results of this will not be limited by the governor. Use this method to retrieve a large number of employee XRefCodes, and then use the GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest class to request employees in batches of 1,000 or less.

GetEmployeeXRefCodesResponse
This class represents the response data returned when submitting a GetEmployeeXRefCodesRequest.

GetReportDefinitionsRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a list of ReportDefinition objects. Report definitions describe reports that are available to be executed by submitting a GetReportRequest object specify the XRefCode of the report.

GetReportPageRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to retrieve a single page of the previously executed report. The response returned will be a Report object.

GetReportRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to execute a report. The response returned will be a Report object.

GetWorkflowValidationDetailRequest
Request object used to query for Workflow details needed to perform validation.

GetWorkflowValidationDetailResponse
Response object for GetWorkflowValidationDetail method.

Job

JobClassification

LDAPSynchronizationFieldListResponse

ListValue
Class which defines a list item that can be used as a report parameter.

OpenReportPagesRequest
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to execute a report and prepare it for retrieval using pagination. The response returned will be a OpenReportPagesResponse object.

OpenReportPagesResponse
This is the response class returned after submitting a OpenReportPagesRequest object. This class contains the information needed to retrieve the report pages and how much data there is.

ReportParameter

ReportParameterDefinition
Report meta data that defines report parameters. Parameter values are supplied by the end-user for execution. All parameters must be supplied during execution. Not all Parameters have default value.

ReportRow

IDayforceService Interface
This interface defines the methods available on the Dayforce Services web service.
Syntax
C#
public interface IDayforceService

The IDayforceService type exposes the following members.
Methods

Name
Description

Authenticate
Authenticates the user and also determines if the user is authorized to use the Dayforce Services API. If successful, a session id is returned which should be passed on subsequent requests to the Execute method.

Execute
Performs a function within the system. This method returns a single result. The function that is executed is based on the type of the DFRequest object that is passed in. If the request object is one which runs a query, only the first item in the query results will be returned to the caller. Typical use of this function is to queue a BJE job, perform clock related functions, or generate a standard Dayforce alert.

GetClientSiteUri
Gets the client site URI which indicates the current site that a client should be using and the service version. The URI returned should point the client at the most recent version of the system that the client is allowed to use.

Logout
Terminates an active session by ending it. This will also attempt to clean up any resources used by the session, such as open report pages associated with the session.

Query
Queries for data within the system. This method returns a list of 0 or more items. The query that is executed is based on the type of DFRequest object that is passed as a parameter.

See Also

IDFNotificationReceiverService Interface
This interface must be implemented by the notification receiver web service. Notification events will be published to the Receive method as events occur.
Syntax
C#
public interface IDFNotificationReceiverService

The IDFNotificationReceiverService type exposes the following members.
Methods

Name
Description

Receive
Receives the specified notification events. Upon receiving an event notification, it should be queued for processing and an acknowledgment immediately returned to the caller.

See Also

CloseReportPagesRequest Class
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to close a previously executed report. This will clean-up all data stored on the server which will help alleviate performance and security issues. The response returned will be a CloseReportPagesResponse object.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.DFRequest

DayforceServiceErrorCode Class
List of error codes that may be returned from Dayforce Services on the DFError class, Code property. The code provided in the documentation can be used if you need it in a client application. 
public class DayforceServiceErrorCode
{
    public static int None = 0;
    public static int UnexpectedError = 1000;
    public static int ConfigurationError = 1001;
    public static int AuthenticationError = 1002;
    public static int AuthorizationError = 1003;
    public static int ValidationError = 1004;
    public static int InvalidSessionError = 1005;
    public static int IpAddressRejected = 1006;
    public static int MaxRecordsExceeded = 1007;
}

Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DayforceServiceErrorCode

Syntax
C#
public class DayforceServiceErrorCode

The DayforceServiceErrorCode type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

DayforceServiceErrorCode

Fields

Name
Description

AuthenticationError
1002 - The credentials could not be authenticated.

AuthorizationError
1003 - The current user is not authorized for the operation requested.

ConfigurationError
1001 - A configuration type error occurred that will require the configuration to be corrected.

InvalidSessionError
1005 - The user session is no longer valid, it most likely timed out. Log in again.

IpAddressRejected
1006 - The IP address the call came from is not allowed.

MaxRecordsExceeded
1007 - The maximum number of records that can be operated on has been exceeded.

None
0 - No error occurred

UnexpectedError
1000 - An unexpected error occurred.

ValidationError
1004 - Data was not in a the proper format.

See Also

Description

DFError

Name
Description

Code

Message
Gets a message that describes the current exception.

StackTrace
Gets a string representation of the frames on the call stack at the time the current exception was thrown.

Employee Class
This is the top level Employee object that is returned on queries for employee data.

  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject

GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest Class
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employees that match a collection of XRefCodes. The results of this query request will be limited in number by the governor setting which is set at 1,000 employees.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.DFRequest
      Dayforce.Services.Data.GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest

Syntax
C#
public class GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest : DFRequest

The GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest

Properties

Name
Description

ContextDate
The Context Date specifies which version of the employee data should be returned. Employees change over time, and this property is used to retrieve employee data as of a particular date. This value defaults to the current date if not specified.

IncludeSubordinateObjects
Use this to control the amount of data returned. A value of True will return all employee data, where as a value of False will return just the top level employee data.

XRefCodes
Array of employee XRef Codes which is used to filter the resulting collection of employees.

See Also

GetEmployeesRequest Class
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employees. The properties on this class are used as filters in the query to restrict the number of employees in the result. The results of this query request will be limited in number by the governor setting which is set at 1,000 employees.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.DFRequest
      Dayforce.Services.Data.GetEmployeesRequest

Syntax
C#
public class GetEmployeesRequest : DFRequest

The GetEmployeesRequest type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

GetEmployeesRequest

Properties

Name
Description

ContextDate
The Context Date specifies which version of the employee data should be returned. Employees change over time, and this property is used to retrieve employee data as of a particular date. This value defaults to the current date if not specified.

EmployeeNumber
Specifying an Employee Number should limit the result to one employee.

EmployeeXRefCode
Specifying an Employee XRef Code will limit the result to one employee.

EmploymentStatus
Filter by employment status groups of Active, Inactive, or Terminated.

FilterHireEndDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been hired on or before the date provided.

FilterHireStartDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been hired on or after the date provided.

FilterTerminationEndDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been terminated on or before the date provided.

FilterTerminationStartDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been terminated on or after the date provided.

IncludeSubordinateObjects
Use this to control the amount of data returned. A value of True will return all employee data, where as a value of False will return just the top level employee data.

OrgUnitXRefCode
Filter by Organization Unit XRefCode

UpdatedAfter
DEPRECATED - Use UpdatedStartDate and UpdatedEndDate.

UpdatedEndDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been updated on or before the date provided.

UpdatedStartDate
If specified, all returned employees will have been updated on or after the date provided.

See Also

GetEmployeeXRefCodesRequest Class
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Query() method to query for a set of employee XRefCodes. This class differs from GetEmployeesRequest in that the results of this will not be limited by the governor. Use this method to retrieve a large number of employee XRefCodes, and then use the GetEmployeesByXRefCodeRequest class to request employees in batches of 1,000 or less.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.DFRequest
      Dayforce.Services.Data.GetEmployeeXRefCodesRequest

OpenReportPagesRequest Class
Submit an instance of this class to the DayforceService.Execute() or DayforceService.Query() method to execute a report and prepare it for retrieval using pagination. The response returned will be a OpenReportPagesResponse object.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.DFRequest
      Dayforce.Services.Data.OpenReportPagesRequest

The OpenReportPagesRequest type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

OpenReportPagesRequest

Properties

Name
Description

PageSize
The size of the pages that the report should be chunked up into. This will determine how much data is returned on each call to retrieve a page.

Parameters
Collection of report parameters to use during the execution of the report.

XRefCode
Reference Code for the Report. This is a unique, human readable, code used to identify the Report.

Description

ReportColumnDefinition Class
This class provides information about a column that is returned as part of a report.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.ReportColumnDefinition

Syntax
C#
public class ReportColumnDefinition : DFObject

The ReportColumnDefinition type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

ReportColumnDefinition

Properties

Name
Description

CodeName
CodeName is a unique name that can be used with code to refer to this specific column. Its value should be consistent.

DataType
This is a string representation of the data type.

DisplayName
This is a name as defined by a user when developing this report. This name would be a human facing name that would be used on a printed report.

Index
Index is a placeholder that represents the position of this column within Report.ColumnDefinitions and Report.Rows[].ColumnValues arrays.

See Also

Constructors

Name
Description

ReportDefinition

Properties

Name
Description

MaxRows
Maximum number of rows the Report will return as part of it's ResultSet. If the MaxRows is assigned -1, it will execute to include all possible rows in it's ResultSet.

Parameters
Collection of report parameters defined by the report.

ReportDescription
Description of the Report. The description will be localized, based on the Session Culture.

ReportName
Name of the Report. The name will be localized, based on the Session Culture.

XRefCode
Reference Code for the Report. This is a unique, human readable, code used to identify the Report.

ReportParameterDefinition Class
Report meta data that defines report parameters. Parameter values are supplied by the end-user for execution. All parameters must be supplied during execution. Not all Parameters have default value.
Inheritance Hierarchy
System.Object
  Dayforce.Services.Data.DFObject
    Dayforce.Services.Data.ReportParameterDefinition

Syntax
C#
public class ReportParameterDefinition : DFObject

The ReportParameterDefinition type exposes the following members.
Constructors

Name
Description

ReportParameterDefinition

Properties

Name
Description

AvailableValues
List of available values a parameter can have.

DataType
Data type of the parameter.

DefaultValue
Default value that will be used if no other value is provided for the parameter. Not all parameters have default value. End-user needs to supply a value in here if the parameter doesn't have value. Reference values should contain Ids and be comma separated. E.g "1,2,3"

DisplayName
Human readable name of the parameter.

IsRequired
True if a value needs to be supplied.

Name
Name of the parameter.

Operator
Operator type of the parameter, such as =, <, >=, etc... Not all parameters have operator type. For example, SQL Parameters don't have operators.

UniqueId
Unique Id of parameter.

See Also
Dayforce.Services.Data Namespace
